I now have enough information to create the answer. Let me compile all the findings:\n\n1. **gcc/passes.def** - Master list of all optimization passes in order of execution. Located in the sg-evals mirror.\n\n2. **gcc/passes.cc** - Implementation of the pass manager that orchestrates pass execution. Contains:\n   - `opt_pass::execute()` - Base implementation of pass execution\n   - `pass_manager::execute_early_local_passes()` - Executes early local optimization passes\n   - `pass_manager::execute_pass_mode_switching()` - Executes mode-switching pass\n   - Macros like NEXT_PASS that connect to pass-instances.def\n\n3. **gcc/pass_manager.h** - Defines the pass manager class and related structures:\n   - `pass_manager` class - Main pass manager\n   - `opt_pass` class (forward declaration) - Base class for all passes\n   - Pass lists: `all_lowering_passes`, `all_small_ipa_passes`, `all_regular_ipa_passes`, `all_late_ipa_passes`, `all_passes`\n\n4. **gcc/tree-pass.h** - Defines pass registration interface and base classes:\n   - `pass_data` struct - Metadata for passes\n   - `opt_pass` class - Base class for all optimization passes with virtual methods: gate(), execute()\n   - `gimple_opt_pass` - Base class for GIMPLE passes\n   - `rtl_opt_pass` - Base class for RTL passes\n   - `ipa_opt_pass_d` - Base class for IPA passes\n   - `simple_ipa_opt_pass` - Base class for simple IPA passes\n   - Pass property and todo flag macros\n\n5. **gcc/tree-ssa-dce.cc** - Concrete implementation of dead code elimination pass:\n   - `pass_data_dce` - Metadata for regular DCE pass\n   - `pass_data_cd_dce` - Metadata for control-dependent DCE pass\n   - `pass_dce_base` - Base class for DCE passes\n   - `pass_dce` and `pass_cd_dce` - Concrete DCE pass classes\n   - `make_pass_dce()` and `make_pass_cd_dce()` - Factory functions to instantiate passes\n   - `perform_tree_ssa_dce()` - Core algorithm implementation\n\n6. **gcc/gen-pass-instances.awk**\n\nAn AWK script that processes passes.def to generate pass-instances.def by adding instance numbers to each pass invocation.
